<Z>Happy New Year <C> Yes, this is the last turn of 2019. Happy New Year to all....<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Late Turns <C> A few reminders and heads-up. Please assume weekend turns will be run either Saturday or Sunday (i.e. please<L.31.1>
don't chase me up Sunday for "missing turns"). I run these games in my spare time, so the more efficient that is the better. <L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Playing Online/Postage Costs <C> 90% of those who play my games now submit orders and receive results via email (both make <L.31.1>
it much easier for me) but I keep the printed option available because a handful of people are really reliant on them to keep <L.31.1>
playing. It'd be much easier (and cheaper, given the average printed turn costs over a quid in terms of stamp, envelope, printer <L.31.1>
toner and paper - and I've not raised turnfees for 20+ years) for me to simply stop doing printed turns, but I want to avoid that. <L.31.1>
However, for those who do still receive turns via the post, you'll see I've now switched to sending these out 2nd class - it<L.31.1>
reduces the cost slightly, but please if you can take results and/or submit orders via the internet, please go in that direction.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>9am Saturday <C> Please note that the deadline is 9am Saturday. It does seem since I've moved that Saturday morning is my<L.31.1>
optimum time for running games, so those who use post please don't send things Friday (delivery is about noon) and those who <L.31.1>
decide to wait until Saturday morning need to be early - there's a few of you who regularly miss the deadline, and in future I<L.31.1>
will simply crack on with games. Equally please don't chase me for "late" results until Monday - although I will generally aim to<L.31.1>
run Sunday, and I'm running the games in my spare time now, it's nice to have some flexibility over the weekend.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Other Games <C> If you aren't aware, I can generally sort out a second (or more) team in a game - I run more than one game of<L.31.1>
Gameplan Baseball, Hoopplan, Slapshot, Raceplan, Run Chase and Gameplan on a fortnightly basis (so I couldn't alternate games on<L.31.1>
different weeks) as well as Gridstats (NFL), Soccer Stats (Premier League) and Play On (AFL Aussie Rules) during their seasons on<L.31.1>
a weekly basis. If you fancy a new, or better, additional challenge, let me know and I can provide details.<L.31.1>
